[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run triggered a critical security issue in Apache Log4j’s [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJndiLookup feature, flagging a “Remote JNDI Lookup” vulnerability that could lead [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto remote code execution or data exfiltration. In response, a patch was proposed [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Updating `core/pom.xml` to add the `org.mockejb:mockejb-jndi:[0m[1;36m2.0[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` test [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependency.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Extending `JndiLookupTest.java` to initialize a mock JNDI context, enable JNDI [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `JndiLookup`, and bind a test object under the standard Log4j JNDI resource [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A Jazzer fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m exercised [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer hook [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flagged a [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` due to a remote JNDI lookup point.  [0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The issue arises from Log4j’s StrSubstitutor invoking `JndiLookup`, which [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms potentially unsafe remote JNDI calls.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness directly logs input that can include JNDI URLs, thereby [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrisks contacting attacker-controlled servers.[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn automated fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJazzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected a critical security issue in Log4j’s [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJndiLookup component: remote JNDI lookups remain enabled by default, allowing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled URLs to trigger code execution or data exfiltration. A proposed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch changes the default `ENABLE_JNDI` flag to `false`, adds setter/getter [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods, adjusts the `lookup` method to return early when lookups are disabled, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduces a MockEJB test dependency plus a unit test. However, when attempting to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapply this patch, the build process failed with a “Permission denied” error on [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/pom.xml`, preventing modification and indicating that the patch did not take [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meffect.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzz test [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggers a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: Remote JNDI Lookup`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows the vulnerability originates in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`, which intercepts calls to [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Downstream, `StrSubstitutor`, `PatternLayout`, and logger appenders invoke the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup, so any log message containing `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` can result in a remote JNDI [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetch.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The default `ENABLE_JNDI = true` in `JndiLookup` allows unbounded JNDI requests, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreating a high-risk attack surface.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `JndiLookup.java`:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Changed `private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI` from `true` to `false`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Added `[0m[1;35msetEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Modified `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to return `null` immediately if JNDI lookups are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabled or `key` is `null`.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Preserved the existing J2EE prefix constant [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `core/pom.xml`:  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Added a test-scope dependency on `org.mockejb:mockejb-jndi:[0m[1;36m2.0[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` to enable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min-JVM JNDI mocking.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `JndiLookupTest.java`:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Imported and enabled JNDI via `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.setEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `@Before`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Configured `MockContextFactory` as the initial JNDI provider.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Bound a test name under the container prefix and verified `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bound value.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
